token","slug":"decrypt-token","term_group":0,"term_taxonomy_id":29319,"taxonomy":"post_tag","description":"","parent":0,"count":7,"filter":"raw","custom_fields":{"i18n":{"hreflang_items":[],"language":{"language_code":"en","locale":"en_US","text_direction":false,"display_name":"English","native_name":"English","different_language":false}},"yoast":{"metatitle":"","metadesc":"","focuskw":null,"linkdex":null,"metakeywords":null,"meta-robots-noindex":null,"meta-robots-nofollow":null,"canonical":null,"redirect":null,"opengraph-title":"","opengraph-description":"","opengraph-image":null,"twitter-title":"","twitter-description":"","twitter-image":null},"authors":[]}}],"link":[]},"content_text":"In this article, well be explaining the mechanics behind how our new token works. Here's everything you want to know about how the tokens are created, how they work, what they can be used for, and why Decrypt created its own reader token.\n\nWHAT IS THE DECRYPT TOKEN?\n\nThe Decrypt Reader Token is used to reward our most loyal and active readers.\n\nIts backed against real cryptocurrency and sent in lightning-fast microtransactions as you read. The token lives inside the Decrypt app, which is available on iOS and Android.\n\nCurrently, the tokens cannot be exchanged for other tokens, or exchanged for fiat.\n\nHOW DO I EARN TOKENS?\n\nEarning tokens couldnt be simpler. Download our app and create a walletit literally takes a few seconds. From that point on, as long as youre logged into your wallet and are in the app, you automatically earn tokens as you read. You can boost your earnings by sharing and reacting to articles.\n[Decrypt Reward Token Drop]\n\nNew tokens are released in seasons. You can see how many are up for grabs at any time in the wallet menu.\n\nWHAT IS A SEASON?\n\nWe partner with great companies to release new batches of tokens into the community. We call this a season.\n\nWe think this is a great way for companies to become an immersive part of the token experience while keeping things exciting for our users.\n\nIn each season there are a limited number of tokens up for grabs, so be quick!\n\nWHAT CAN I DO WITH THE DECRYPT TOKEN?\n\nThe Decrypt token can be used to redeem rewards on the Decrypt reward store. You can find the reward store inside the app.\n\nDuring our first season, users who've amassed enough tokens can swap them for super limited NFTs created by some of our favorite artists. But we plan on offering a lot more than that as our token evolves. Each season will feature something new so keep checking in to see whats on offer.\n\n[Decrypt Token daily cap UI]\n\nTo redeem your tokens click on the Rewards button on the wallet menu.\n\nIn the future, Decrypt drops will evolve to include a host of different rewards and different functionality. So stay tuned.\n\nWHY IS DECRYPT INTRODUCING A TOKEN?\n\nAt Decrypt weve always been firm believers that the technology we write about every day should be a core part of our DNA.\n\nWe believe that applying Web3 technology in thoughtful and engaging ways can help us tell better stories and also be a step toward solving some of medias biggest problems.\n\n The reader token is a natural progression of our mission to demystify the decentralized web. With our token we can now introduce those readers to the core concepts of cryptocurrencies: wallets, balances, transactions. \n\nWe believe there is a better way for media companies to bring together audiences, publishers, and advertisers in a way where everyone can benefit. The Decrypt Reader Token is the first step in that journey.\n\nWHAT PROBLEM DOES THE DECRYPT TOKEN SOLVE?\n\nWe believe it's essential for the media industry to create better relationships between readers and advertisers. Tokens can help unlock new and better ways for media companies to thrive.\n\nTwo of the leading reasons users want a connection to a brand is a sense of ownership and the opportunity for rewards.\n\nWe like to think of the Decrypt Reader Token as a tool to build a more engaged community of readers.\n\nHOW DOES ALL THIS WORK?\n\nThe Decrypt Reader Token is built on OpenST, an open-source token platform. This allows us to ensure that the wallet is totally non-custodial. That means you have full ownership and control over your tokens. All keys are stored on your mobile device. Decrypt cant see or control that password.\n\nAll the transactions that happen in the background while you read take place on Ethereum, the leading platform for blockchain applications.\n\nhttps://www.youtube.com/watch?v=d1Lqeb6g15k\n\nWhen you complete an earn action, we transfer tokens from the Decrypt reserve to your wallet. We do this through an \"Ethereum sidechain\" to achieve fast and extremely low-cost microtransactions.\n\nAt the moment, the tokens cannot be exchanged for other tokens, or exchanged for fiat.\n\nTHE FUTURE\n\nOur initial implementation of the Decrypt Reader Token is designed to be simple, fun, and engaging. We have lots of plans to make the token more useful to our community of users, while helping Decrypt to improve and support its journalism.\n\nWe have a Discord channel we use to keep people updated on whats happening with the Decrypt Reader Token. If youre interested in keeping up to date with the Decrypt token, join our Discord server. \n","read_this_next_post_id":5736,"read_this_next_post_type":"post","social_share_img_url":"https://cdn.decrypt.co/resize/1024/height/512/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Decrypt-Token-v2-1-gID_4-pID_3.png","featured_image_caption":"","featured_image_description":"","featured_image_url":"https://cdn.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Decrypt-Token-v2-1-gID_4-pID_3.png","primary_category":{"term_id":23624,"name":"Learn","slug":"learn","term_group":0,"term_taxonomy_id":23624,"taxonomy":"category","description":"The World of Blockchain \u0026amp; Cryptocurrencies made simple.","parent":0,"count":0,"filter":"raw"}}},{"id":20427,"date":"2021-03-19T09:02:47","date_gmt":"2021-03-19T09:02:47","guid":{"rendered":"https://wp.decrypt.co/?p=20427"},"modified":"2021-03-19T13:12:34","modified_gmt":"2021-03-19T13:12:34","slug":"what-is-secret-network-scrt-formerly-enigma","status":"publish","type":"post","link":"https://wp.decrypt.co/20427/what-is-secret-network-scrt-formerly-enigma/","title":{"rendered":"What is Secret Network (SCRT)?"},"content":{"rendered":"\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eBlockchain technology provides a beneficial layer of openness and transparency that current centralized networks cannot, but some private data isnt meant to be shared publicly.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eHow many people want to use a network that shares their financial details and identifying information to everyone, for example?\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eThats the issue that Secret Network aims to solve. By enabling programmable smart contracts that run on blockchain and compute within trusted execution environments, shielding the data from the nodes themselves, Secret Network promises the transparent benefits of blockchain with the kind of security and privacy that users demand from web services.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eHeres a look at how Secret Network works and what the community behind it hopes to achieve with the project.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cb\u003eWhat is Secret Network?\u003c/b\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eSecret Network is a blockchain built specifically for data privacy. By supporting encrypted inputs, outputs, and smart contract states, Secret Network enables programmable smart contracts that keep user data safe. If coins like Monero and Zcash are the privacy-centric evolution of Bitcoin, Secret Networks smart contracts are like an evolution of Ethereums own smart contracts, building upon that premise while enabling the secure transfer of private data.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eSecret Network was born out of Enigma, a startup that developed the concept of a decentralized protocol for secret smart contracts. Enigma raised $45 million in a 2017 initial coin offering (ICO), but \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/19993/sec-drops-the-hammer-on-enigmas-45-million-ico\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003efaced enforcement\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003e from the United States Securities and Exchange Commission in 2020 that forced a settlement with the SEC.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eUltimately, the community around Enigma decided to continue that vision as an independent, decentralized project, which is how the \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://blog.enigma.co/introducing-secret-network-ed48621754ad\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"nofollow external noopener\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003ecurrent version of Secret Network was born\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003e. A swap allowed holders of Enigmas Ethereum-based ENG token to trade 1:1 for SCRT, the native coin of Secret Network used for governance and paying fees. Enigma remains involved as one of the key players in the community supporting development of Secret Network.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ciframe title=\"Introducing Secret Network - in Sixty Seconds\" width=\"640\" height=\"360\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/c70BBVUCxxk?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen\u003e\u003c/iframe\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cb\u003eHow does Secret Network work?\u003c/b\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eSecret Network is a layer-1 blockchain with its own consensus and on-chain governance, built atop the \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/resources/cosmos\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eCosmos\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003e/Tendermint framework\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003e. It relies on a network of distributed nodes that perform the computation of smart contracts built on Secret Network, but the nodes use a trusted execution environment (TEE)like a black boxto do so away from prying eyes.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eIts similar to how a smartphone processor uses a TEE to handle sensitive data like fingerprints, but its a blockchain node instead. The network bills its smart contracts as secret contracts, as theyre designed to preserve the privacy of the data held within. The SCRT (Secret) coin must be staked by nodes to participate in the network, plus it is used to pay fees and transfer value.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"did-you-know\"\u003eAs part of the 2020 settlement, the SEC forced Enigma to offer refunds to investors, register its token as a security, and pay a $500,000 fine.\u003c/div\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cb\u003eWhats so special about Secret Network?\u003c/b\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eTheres a lot to like about blockchains as far as being immutable and transparent, but that kind of openness limits the kind of data that can be safely handled by many blockchainsparticularly top-secret data that people or companies wouldnt want seen by just anyone.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eSecret Network aims to plug that hole by providing the layer of privacy and security while still keeping what people like about blockchain technologythe best of both worlds, in theory. While its not the only company attempting to fill that void, its a concept that could be key to driving the future of certain decentralized apps (\u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/resources/dapps\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003edapps\u003c/a\u003e), particularly in the realm of decentralized finance (\u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/resources/defi-ultimate-beginners-guide-decentralized-finance\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eDeFi\u003c/a\u003e).\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003e\u003cb\u003eWhat can you do with Secret Network?\u003c/b\u003e\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eSecret Network is designed to empower decentralized applications that demand a level of privacy not found on many other blockchain networks. By using a trusted execution environment and keeping private data away from both the public and node operators, it can handle sensitive information that users and organizations might not otherwise be willing to share.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eThe networks operators have proposed a wide number of potential use cases, including credit scoring and lending dapps that ensure privacy, machine learning capabilities that still retain privacy in the process, and improving the ability to safely share and monetize data. More widely, Secret Network could potentially be useful to any dapp that handles sensitive data.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"did-you-know\"\u003eCosmos, the framework Secret Network is built on, is billed as the internet of blockchains and aims to create an interconnected ecosystem of blockchains, whereas many current blockchains are like individual silos.\u003c/div\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote class=\"twitter-tweet\" data-width=\"550\" data-dnt=\"true\"\u003e\n\u003cp lang=\"en\" dir=\"ltr\"\u003eNEW Update! A lack of cross-chain compatibility could limit Secret Networks appeal and ultimately keep it from being as widespread or useful as the community developers intend it to be.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eSecret Network is also making a big decentralized finance push with its \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://scrt.network/blog/secret-defi-sefi-genesis-secretswap\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"nofollow external noopener\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eSecret DeFi\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003e initiative, and launched a SecretSwap decentralized exchange in February 2021. According to the \u003c/span\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://scrt.network/about/about-secret-network\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"nofollow external noopener\"\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eSecret Network FAQ\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003e, part of our vision has always been bringing privacy to \u003c/span\u003e\u003ci\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eevery\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/i\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003e blockchain, and it calls out Cosmos inter-blockchain communication and interoperability as another potential initiative on the roadmap.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan style=\"font-weight: 400;\"\u003eBeyond that, Secret Network appears focused on attracting more developers to build their dapps on the blockchain, thus demonstrating more use cases in the process. Network","slug":"secret-network","term_group":0,"term_taxonomy_id":33176,"taxonomy":"post_tag","description":"","parent":0,"count":1,"filter":"raw","custom_fields":{"i18n":{"hreflang_items":[],"language":{"language_code":"en","locale":"en_US","text_direction":false,"display_name":"English","native_name":"English","different_language":false}},"yoast":{"metatitle":"","metadesc":"","focuskw":null,"linkdex":null,"metakeywords":null,"meta-robots-noindex":null,"meta-robots-nofollow":null,"canonical":null,"redirect":null,"opengraph-title":"","opengraph-description":"","opengraph-image":null,"twitter-title":"","twitter-description":"","twitter-image":null},"authors":[]}}],"link":[]},"content_text":"Blockchain technology provides a beneficial layer of openness and transparency that current centralized networks cannot, but some private data isnt meant to be shared publicly.\n\nHow many people want to use a network that shares their financial details and identifying information to everyone, for example?\n\nThats the issue that Secret Network aims to solve. By enabling programmable smart contracts that run on blockchain and compute within trusted execution environments, shielding the data from the nodes themselves, Secret Network promises the transparent benefits of blockchain with the kind of security and privacy that users demand from web services.\n\nHeres a look at how Secret Network works and what the community behind it hopes to achieve with the project.\n\nWHAT IS SECRET NETWORK?\n\nSecret Network is a blockchain built specifically for data privacy. By supporting encrypted inputs, outputs, and smart contract states, Secret Network enables programmable smart contracts that keep user data safe. If coins like Monero and Zcash are the privacy-centric evolution of Bitcoin, Secret Networks smart contracts are like an evolution of Ethereums own smart contracts, building upon that premise while enabling the secure transfer of private data.\n\nSecret Network was born out of Enigma, a startup that developed the concept of a decentralized protocol for secret smart contracts. Enigma raised $45 million in a 2017 initial coin offering (ICO), but faced enforcement from the United States Securities and Exchange Commission in 2020 that forced a settlement with the SEC.\n\nUltimately, the community around Enigma decided to continue that vision as an independent, decentralized project, which is how the current version of Secret Network was born. A swap allowed holders of Enigmas Ethereum-based ENG token to trade 1:1 for SCRT, the native coin of Secret Network used for governance and paying fees. Enigma remains involved as one of the key players in the community supporting development of Secret Network.\n\nHOW DOES SECRET NETWORK WORK?\n\nSecret Network is a layer-1 blockchain with its own consensus and on-chain governance, built atop the Cosmos/Tendermint framework. It relies on a network of distributed nodes that perform the computation of smart contracts built on Secret Network, but the nodes use a trusted execution environment (TEE)like a black boxto do so away from prying eyes.\n\nIts similar to how a smartphone processor uses a TEE to handle sensitive data like fingerprints, but its a blockchain node instead. The network bills its smart contracts as secret contracts, as theyre designed to preserve the privacy of the data held within. The SCRT (Secret) coin must be staked by nodes to participate in the network, plus it is used to pay fees and transfer value.\n\n As part of the 2020 settlement, the SEC forced Enigma to offer refunds to investors, register its token as a security, and pay a $500,000 fine.\n\nWHATS SO SPECIAL ABOUT SECRET NETWORK?\n\nTheres a lot to like about blockchains as far as being immutable and transparent, but that kind of openness limits the kind of data that can be safely handled by many blockchainsparticularly top-secret data that people or companies wouldnt want seen by just anyone.\n\nSecret Network aims to plug that hole by providing the layer of privacy and security while still keeping what people like about blockchain technologythe best of both worlds, in theory. While its not the only company attempting to fill that void, its a concept that could be key to driving the future of certain decentralized apps (dapps), particularly in the realm of decentralized finance (DeFi).\n\nWHAT CAN YOU DO WITH SECRET NETWORK?\n\nSecret Network is designed to empower decentralized applications that demand a level of privacy not found on many other blockchain networks. By using a trusted execution environment and keeping private data away from both the public and node operators, it can handle sensitive information that users and organizations might not otherwise be willing to share.\n\nThe networks operators have proposed a wide number of potential use cases, including credit scoring and lending dapps that ensure privacy, machine learning capabilities that still retain privacy in the process, and improving the ability to safely share and monetize data. More widely, Secret Network could potentially be useful to any dapp that handles sensitive data.\n\n Cosmos, the framework Secret Network is built on, is billed as the internet of blockchains and aims to create an interconnected ecosystem of blockchains, whereas many current blockchains are like individual silos.\n\n\u003eNEWUpdate!$SEFI,nativegovernancetokenforSecretDeFi,nowhasagenesisdate:March31st,2021.\n\u003e\n\u003eInthisblog:howyoucanreceive$SEFI,recent@secret_swapgrowthandimprovements,upcomingbridges(including#BSCandbeyond),andmore!$SCRThttps://t.co/GCxGf8T30B\n\u003e\n\u003eecretNetwork(@SecretNetwork)March17,2021\n\nTHE FUTURE FOR SCRT\n\nWith the ENG-to-SCRT token swap concluding in January 2021, effectively closing the book on the old Enigma project, Secret Network is trying to build towards a future that embraces interoperability with other blockchains. A lack of cross-chain compatibility could limit Secret Networks appeal and ultimately keep it from being as widespread or useful as the community developers intend it to be.\n\nSecret Network is also making a big decentralized finance push with its Secret DeFi initiative, and launched a SecretSwap decentralized exchange in February 2021. According to the Secret Network FAQ, part of our vision has always been bringing privacy to _every_ blockchain, and it calls out Cosmos inter-blockchain communication and interoperability as another potential initiative on the roadmap.\n\nBeyond that, Secret Network appears focused on attracting more developers to build their dapps on the blockchain, thus demonstrating more use cases in the process. Its not the only blockchain with privacy-focused smart contracts (Oasis Network is another example) and there are other potential solutions to the dilemma of handling sensitive data on blockchainsuch as secure multi-party computation. Whether Secret Networks solution ultimately stands above others currently on the market or even on the horizon remains to be seen.\n","read_this_next_post_id":"19993","read_this_next_post_type":"post","social_share_img_url":"https://cdn.decrypt.co/resize/1024/height/512/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/Image-from-iOS-1-gID_5-pID_4.png","featured_image_caption":"","featured_image_description":"","featured_image_url":"https://cdn.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2020/02/Image-from-iOS-1-gID_5-pID_4.png","primary_category":{"term_id":23624,"name":"Learn","slug":"learn","term_group":0,"term_taxonomy_id":23624,"taxonomy":"category","description":"The World of Blockchain \u0026amp; Cryptocurrencies made simple.","parent":0,"count":0,"filter":"raw"}}},{"id":61000,"date":"2021-03-18T17:45:36","date_gmt":"2021-03-18T17:45:36","guid":{"rendered":"https://wp.decrypt.co/?p=61000"},"modified":"2021-03-18T17:45:32","modified_gmt":"2021-03-18T17:45:32","slug":"what-is-nba-top-shot-a-beginners-guide-2021","status":"publish","type":"post","link":"https://wp.decrypt.co/61000/what-is-nba-top-shot-a-beginners-guide-2021/","title":{"rendered":"What is NBA Top Shot? A Beginners Guide (2021)"},"content":{"rendered":"\u003cp\u003eNBA Top Shot is the latest crypto collectibles craze, in which the most iconic moments in NBA history are turned into non-fungible tokens, or \u003cspan class=\"link\"\u003e\u003ca alt=\"What are NFTs?\" href=\"https://decrypt.co/resources/non-fungible-tokens-nfts-explained-guide-learn-blockchain\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eNFTs\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/span\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAn NFT is a special type of cryptocurrency token thats cryptographically uniquemeaning that, like physical collectibles such as trading cards, they have a limited supply. And theyre becoming a worldwide phenomenonwith NBA Top Shot leading the way.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cfigure id=\"attachment_61005\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-61005\" style=\"width: 1920px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"\u003e\u003cimg loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-61005 size-full\" src=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/3D-Top-Shot-Logo.png\" alt=\"NBA Top Shot logo\" width=\"1920\" height=\"1080\" srcset=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/3D-Top-Shot-Logo.png 1920w, https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/3D-Top-Shot-Logo-300x169.png 300w, https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/3D-Top-Shot-Logo-768x432.png 768w, https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/3D-Top-Shot-Logo-1536x864.png 1536w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1920px) 100vw, 1920px\" /\u003e\u003cfigcaption id=\"caption-attachment-61005\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"\u003eNBA Top Shot lets you collect basketball moments. Image: NBA Top Shot.\u003c/figcaption\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn the last month alone, 100,000 people have purchased NBA Top Shot moments, according to data provider \u003ca href=\"https://www.cryptoslam.io/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" rel=\"nofollow external noopener\"\u003eCryptoSlam\u003c/a\u003e, either hoping to possess their stars favorite jump shot or to make money by selling it for a higher price.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWith the increased attention, prices for NBA Top Shots are rising. Current prices range from $14 for a Rudy Gay dunk to $240,000 for a Ja Morant dunk.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eWhat are NBA Top Shot collectibles?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eNBA Top Shot is the biggest mainstream example of digital collectible cards. You can think of them as trading cards, but instead of being printed on card, theyre kept on a blockchain. This means you can keep them in your digital wallet and send them to other people, or sell them in online marketplaces.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach Top Shot features a moment from basketball history, in the form of a short video clip.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote class=\"twitter-tweet\" data-width=\"550\" data-dnt=\"true\"\u003e\n\u003cp lang=\"en\" dir=\"ltr\"\u003eMetallic Gold LE Challenge 19 expires in 24 hours \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCollectors have until Friday, March 19 at 10am PDT to acquire all 9 required Moments to score this exclusive reward of Terry Rozier throwing down a vicious  over KD \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eMore info: \u003ca href=\"https://t.co/Rkg3ro7D3t\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003ehttps://t.co/Rkg3ro7D3t\u003c/a\u003e \u003ca href=\"https://t.co/m3Db0aWGKK\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003epic.twitter.com/m3Db0aWGKK\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026mdash; NBA Top Shot (@nbatopshot) \u003ca href=\"https://twitter.com/nbatopshot/status/1372593642708332545?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eMarch 18, 2021\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cscript async src=\"https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"\u003e\u003c/script\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSimilar to trading cards, there are multiple cards for each moment. Packs are released in various sizes, with smaller packs increasing the rarity of the cards. The common tier includes packs that have 10,000 cards or more. The rare tier has packs of 150-4,999 cards and the legendary tier limits them to 25-499 cards.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWithin each pack, each card has its own serial number. But these can cause prices to vary wildly. For example, for a \u003ca href=\"https://www.nbatopshot.com/listings/p2p/208ae30a-a4fe-42d4-9e51-e6fd1ad2a7a9+770334d2-0397-43d0-8ca8-3fee16822821\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eJayson Tatum jump shot\u003c/a\u003e, the lowest ask is $52; the highest sale, for serial #5206, $28,000. Thats a huge discrepancy for the same cardsomething to bear in mind if youre looking to resell the cards.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cfigure id=\"attachment_61011\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-61011\" style=\"width: 445px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"\u003e\u003cimg loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-61011 size-full\" src=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.24.15.png\" alt=\"Jayson Tatum shooting hoops\" width=\"445\" height=\"359\" srcset=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.24.15.png 445w, https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.24.15-300x242.png 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 445px) 100vw, 445px\" /\u003e\u003cfigcaption id=\"caption-attachment-61011\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"\u003eA Jayson Tatum assist. Image: NBA Top Shot.\u003c/figcaption\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThere are multiple trading sets too. The For The Win series comprises 10 specific moments from one of Spencer Dinwiddies jump shots to a Nemanja Bjelica three-pointer. They are all rare cards.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eCreating an account with Dapper Labs\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUnlike traditional trading cards, these collectibles arent printed out on paper and sold in physical stores. Rather, NBA Top Shot cards are stored on the Flow blockchain, which was built by Dapper Labs (the team behind early NFT phenomenon CryptoKitties). So theyre a little bit more complicated to get hold of.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo get started, youll need to register for NBA Top Shot with Dapper. You can do this by clicking sign up on the Top Shot website. Creating a Dapper account gives you a wallet that stores funds and enables you to purchase crypto collectibles.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cfigure id=\"attachment_61015\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-61015\" style=\"width: 425px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"\u003e\u003cimg loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-61015 size-full\" src=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.26.21.png\" alt=\"Signing up for Dapper\" width=\"425\" height=\"515\" srcset=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.26.21.png 425w, https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.26.21-248x300.png 248w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 425px) 100vw, 425px\" /\u003e\u003cfigcaption id=\"caption-attachment-61015\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"\u003eHow to sign up for Dapper. Image: Dapper Labs.\u003c/figcaption\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eRegistering with Dapper is straightforward. You sign in via Google or email, then provide your telephone number and verify it. Dapper then provides you with a code that you need to keep safely in case you lose access via the device youre on. Its important to write this down somewhere and keep it in a safe place, as it controls access to your account.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eGetting started with NBA Top Shot\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eOnce youve registered with Dapper, you can go straight to NBA Top Shot and use the account to sign in.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe first time you sign in, youll be greeted with a couple of introductory videos, before youre asked if you want to join the NBA Top Shot Discord channel. Then youll be able to select which team you support.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cfigure id=\"attachment_61018\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-61018\" style=\"width: 1284px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"\u003e\u003cimg loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-61018 size-full\" src=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.29.24.png\" alt=\"Choosing your basketball team\" width=\"1284\" height=\"404\" srcset=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.29.24.png 1284w, https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.29.24-300x94.png 300w, https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.29.24-768x242.png 768w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 1284px) 100vw, 1284px\" /\u003e\u003cfigcaption id=\"caption-attachment-61018\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"\u003eYou can choose your favorite team. Image: NBA Top Shot.\u003c/figcaption\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eOnce youre in, you will see your randomly generated username. You can easily change this by clicking change username, going to your Dapper Labs profile and choosing something that suits you better.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eNow you can explore the packs on offer (which will typically be sold out!) and the marketplace where you can buy trading cards second hand. But in order to buy anything, youll need some funds.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eLoading up your account\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIn order to buy an NBA Top Shot moment, youll need to put some funds into your Dapper account.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou can do this by going to Payment and Payouts on the site. Here, you choose how much you want to put into your account; youll have to agree to Dappers terms and conditions. Then you can either pay with a credit card, by entering your details, or with cryptocurrency. Dapper accepts \u003cspan class=\"link\"\u003e\u003ca alt=\"bitcoin news\" href=\"https://decrypt.co/crypto-news/bitcoin\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eBitcoin\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"link\"\u003e\u003ca alt=\"More about Ethereum\" href=\"https://decrypt.co/crypto-news/ethereum\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eEthereum\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"link\"\u003e\u003ca alt=\"More about Bitcoin Cash\" href=\"https://decrypt.co/crypto-news/bitcoin-cash\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eBitcoin Cash\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/span\u003e and two stablecoins: DAI and USDC.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cfigure id=\"attachment_61021\" aria-describedby=\"caption-attachment-61021\" style=\"width: 507px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"\u003e\u003cimg loading=\"lazy\" class=\"wp-image-61021 size-full\" src=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.37.51.png\" alt=\"Adding money to your account\" width=\"507\" height=\"531\" srcset=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.37.51.png 507w, https://wp.decrypt.co/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Screenshot-2021-03-11-at-17.37.51-286x300.png 286w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 507px) 100vw, 507px\" /\u003e\u003cfigcaption id=\"caption-attachment-61021\" class=\"wp-caption-text\"\u003eHow to add funds to your Dapper account. Image: Dapper Labs.\u003c/figcaption\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eOnce youve loaded up your account with funds, you may need to wait for them to land in your wallet (cryptocurrencies can sometimes be a bit slow) before theyre ready to spend. You will also have to pay network fees when making a cryptocurrency transaction, so make sure to check how much that will cost and account for it (Bitcoin fees are currently around $13 per transaction).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsing the NBA Top Shot marketplace\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe marketplace can be a bit overwhelming, because there are thousands of Top Shot cardsbut there are ways to narrow down the list. You can select moments for specific teams or players, and you can rank the cards by price.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eIf you want to purchase a card, you will need to find the moment you like and select the serial number of the specific card. Then you click purchase and you can pay with the funds in your Dapper account.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAfter that, what can you do with them? Well, you can store the cards and watch the moments when you want. You can then put them up for sale, or, if youre generous enough, you can gift them to a friend. Top Shot","slug":"nba-top-shot","term_group":0,"term_taxonomy_id":30492,"taxonomy":"post_tag","description":"","parent":0,"count":14,"filter":"raw","custom_fields":{"i18n":{"hreflang_items":[],"language":{"language_code":"en","locale":"en_US","text_direction":false,"display_name":"English","native_name":"English","different_language":false}},"yoast":{"metatitle":"","metadesc":"","focuskw":null,"linkdex":null,"metakeywords":null,"meta-robots-noindex":null,"meta-robots-nofollow":null,"canonical":null,"redirect":null,"opengraph-title":"","opengraph-description":"","opengraph-image":null,"twitter-title":"","twitter-description":"","twitter-image":null},"authors":[]}},{"term_id":26608,"name":"NFT","slug":"nft","term_group":0,"term_taxonomy_id":26608,"taxonomy":"post_tag","description":"","parent":0,"count":174,"filter":"raw","custom_fields":{"i18n":{"hreflang_items":[],"language":{"language_code":"en","locale":"en_US","text_direction":false,"display_name":"English","native_name":"English","different_language":false}},"yoast":{"metatitle":"","metadesc":"","focuskw":null,"linkdex":null,"metakeywords":null,"meta-robots-noindex":null,"meta-robots-nofollow":null,"canonical":null,"redirect":null,"opengraph-title":"","opengraph-description":"","opengraph-image":null,"twitter-title":"","twitter-description":"","twitter-image":null},"authors":[]}},{"term_id":28708,"name":"Tokens","slug":"tokens","term_group":0,"term_taxonomy_id":28708,"taxonomy":"post_tag","description":"","parent":0,"count":14,"filter":"raw","custom_fields":{"i18n":{"hreflang_items":[],"language":{"language_code":"en","locale":"en_US","text_direction":false,"display_name":"English","native_name":"English","different_language":false}},"yoast":{"metatitle":"","metadesc":"","focuskw":null,"linkdex":null,"metakeywords":null,"meta-robots-noindex":null,"meta-robots-nofollow":null,"canonical":null,"redirect":null,"opengraph-title":"","opengraph-description":"","opengraph-image":null,"twitter-title":"","twitter-description":"","twitter-image":null},"authors":[]}}],"link":[]},"content_text":"NBA Top Shot is the latest crypto collectibles craze, in which the most iconic moments in NBA history are turned into non-fungible tokens, or NFTs.\n\nAn NFT is a special type of cryptocurrency token thats cryptographically uniquemeaning that, like physical collectibles such as trading cards, they have a limited supply. And theyre becoming a worldwide phenomenonwith NBA Top Shot leading the way.\n[NBA Top Shot logo]NBA Top Shot lets you collect basketball moments. Image: NBA Top Shot.\nIn the last month alone, 100,000 people have purchased NBA Top Shot moments, according to data provider CryptoSlam, either hoping to possess their stars favorite jump shot or to make money by selling it for a higher price.\n\nWith the increased attention, prices for NBA Top Shots are rising. Current prices range from $14 for a Rudy Gay dunk to $240,000 for a Ja Morant dunk.\n\nWHAT ARE NBA TOP SHOT COLLECTIBLES?\n\nNBA Top Shot is the biggest mainstream example of digital collectible cards. You can think of them as trading cards, but instead of being printed on card, theyre kept on a blockchain. This means you can keep them in your digital wallet and send them to other people, or sell them in online marketplaces.\n\nEach Top Shot features a moment from basketball history, in the form of a short video clip.\n\n\u003eMetallicGoldLEChallenge19expiresin24hours\n\u003e\n\u003eCollectorshaveuntilFriday,March19at10amPDTtoacquireall9requiredMomentstoscorethisexclusiverewardofTerryRozierthrowingdownaviciousoverKD\n\u003e\n\u003eMoreinfo:https://t.co/Rkg3ro7D3tpic.twitter.com/m3Db0aWGKK\n\u003e\n\u003eNBATopShot(@nbatopshot)March18,2021\n\nSimilar to trading cards, there are multiple cards for each moment. Packs are released in various sizes, with smaller packs increasing the rarity of the cards. The common tier includes packs that have 10,000 cards or more. The rare tier has packs of 150-4,999 cards and the legendary tier limits them to 25-499 cards.\n\nWithin each pack, each card has its own serial number. But these can cause prices to vary wildly. For example, for a Jayson Tatum jump shot, the lowest ask is $52; the highest sale, for serial #5206, $28,000. Thats a huge discrepancy for the same cardsomething to bear in mind if youre looking to resell the cards.\n[Jayson Tatum shooting hoops]A Jayson Tatum assist. Image: NBA Top Shot.\nThere are multiple trading sets too. The For The Win series comprises 10 specific moments from one of Spencer Dinwiddies jump shots to a Nemanja Bjelica three-pointer. They are all rare cards.\n\nCREATING AN ACCOUNT WITH DAPPER LABS\n\nUnlike traditional trading cards, these collectibles arent printed out on paper and sold in physical stores. Rather, NBA Top Shot cards are stored on the Flow blockchain, which was built by Dapper Labs (the team behind early NFT phenomenon CryptoKitties). So theyre a little bit more complicated to get hold of.\n\nTo get started, youll need to register for NBA Top Shot with Dapper. You can do this by clicking sign up on the Top Shot website. Creating a Dapper account gives you a wallet that stores funds and enables you to purchase crypto collectibles.\n[Signing up for Dapper]How to sign up for Dapper. Image: Dapper Labs.\nRegistering with Dapper is straightforward. You sign in via Google or email, then provide your telephone number and verify it. Dapper then provides you with a code that you need to keep safely in case you lose access via the device youre on. Its important to write this down somewhere and keep it in a safe place, as it controls access to your account.\n\nGETTING STARTED WITH NBA TOP SHOT\n\nOnce youve registered with Dapper, you can go straight to NBA Top Shot and use the account to sign in.\n\nThe first time you sign in, youll be greeted with a couple of introductory videos, before youre asked if you want to join the NBA Top Shot Discord channel. Then youll be able to select which team you support.\n[Choosing your basketball team]You can choose your favorite team. Image: NBA Top Shot.\nOnce youre in, you will see your randomly generated username. You can easily change this by clicking change username, going to your Dapper Labs profile and choosing something that suits you better.\n\nNow you can explore the packs on offer (which will typically be sold out!) and the marketplace where you can buy trading cards second hand. But in order to buy anything, youll need some funds.\n\nLOADING UP YOUR ACCOUNT\n\nIn order to buy an NBA Top Shot moment, youll need to put some funds into your Dapper account.\n\nYou can do this by going to Payment and Payouts on the site. Here, you choose how much you want to put into your account; youll have to agree to Dappers terms and conditions. Then you can either pay with a credit card, by entering your details, or with cryptocurrency. Dapper accepts Bitcoin, Ethereum, Bitcoin Cash and two stablecoins: DAI and USDC.\n[Adding money to your account]How to add funds to your Dapper account. Image: Dapper Labs.\nOnce youve loaded up your account with funds, you may need to wait for them to land in your wallet (cryptocurrencies can sometimes be a bit slow) before theyre ready to spend. You will also have to pay network fees when making a cryptocurrency transaction, so make sure to check how much that will cost and account for it (Bitcoin fees are currently around $13 per transaction).\n\nUSING THE NBA TOP SHOT MARKETPLACE\n\nThe marketplace can be a bit overwhelming, because there are thousands of Top Shot cardsbut there are ways to narrow down the list. You can select moments for specific teams or players, and you can rank the cards by price.\n\nIf you want to purchase a card, you will need to find the moment you like and select the serial number of the specific card. Then you click purchase and you can pay with the funds in your Dapper account.\n\nAfter that, what can you do with them? Well, you can store the cards and watch the moments when you want. You can then put them up for sale, or, if youre generous enough, you can gift them to a friend. What you _cant _do is use the footage in the Top Shot yourself, or modify the image without permissionin fact, the NBAs lawyers have put together a laundry list of prohibitions restricting what you can do with their costly IP.\n","read_this_next_post_id":61565,"read_this_next_post_type":"post","social_share_img_url":"https://cdn.decrypt.co/resize/1024/height/512/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/nba-top-shot-basketball-gID_5-pID_5.png","featured_image_caption":"NBA Top Shot. href=\"https://decrypt.co/crypto-news/ethereum\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eEthereum\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/span\u003e blockchain to a halt in late 2017 due to immense congestion, developer Dapper charset=\"utf-8\"\u003e\u003c/script\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCryptoKitties \u003ca href=\"https://www.cryptokitties.co/blog/post/cryptokitties-on-flow/\" href=\"https://decrypt.co/60808/so-you-bought-an-nba-top-shot-nft-what-do-you-actually-own\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eNBA Top Shot\u003c/a\u003e, and many other developers signing on to build with Flow amidst the \u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/59968/nft-mania-february-trading-volume-just-topped-all-2020\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eNFT boom\u003c/a\u003e, it could prove to be one of the leading blockchains for such creations.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eHeres a look at what Flow is, how it works, and how to get ahold of the FLOW token.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eWhat is Flow?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFlow is a blockchain that is designed for extensive scaling without the use of \u003cspan class=\"definition\" link=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/?post_type=post\u0026p=5696\" slug=\"sharding\"\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://wp.decrypt.co/?post_type=post\u0026amp;p=5696\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003esharding\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/span\u003e techniques, providing fast and low-cost transactions that make sense for dapps such as NFT marketplaces and crypto-infused video games.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eAs mentioned, Flow hails from Dapper Labs, which decided to solve its blockchain congestion problem head-on by building one primed for games and other interactive experiences. Dapper is now using Flow for all of its own projects, including NBA Top Shot, but its open to other developers as well.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote class=\"twitter-tweet\" data-width=\"550\" data-dnt=\"true\"\u003e\n\u003cp lang=\"en\" dir=\"ltr\"\u003eFlow is split into FOUR node types to achieve dramatic improvements in speed and throughput\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e1 Collector Nodes increase efficiency\u003cbr /\u003e2 Execution Nodes enable speed and scale\u003cbr /\u003e3 Verifier Nodes guarantee correctness\u003cbr /\u003e4 Consensus Nodes ensure decentralization\u003ca href=\"https://t.co/8zFlufRONm\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003ehttps://t.co/8zFlufRONm\u003c/a\u003e \u003ca href=\"https://t.co/7FJoEKSi7K\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003epic.twitter.com/7FJoEKSi7K\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026mdash; Flow Blockchain (@flow_blockchain) \u003ca href=\"https://twitter.com/flow_blockchain/status/1335670548391587840?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eDecember 6, 2020\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cscript async src=\"https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"\u003e\u003c/script\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eHow does Flow work?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFlow uses a \u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/resources/concensus\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eproof-of-stake\u003c/a\u003e model that requires validators to stake a certain number of FLOW tokens to participate in the network.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eHowever, the way that validation works is unique amongst blockchains as Flow splits validation tasks into four separate types of nodes: consensus, verification, execution, and collection. All four node types participate in the validation of each transaction.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eDapper says that splitting up the tasks makes processing transactions more efficient than on rival blockchains. Its an alternative option to sharding, or spreading out the storage and computational needs of a blockchain across numerous nodes. Flow does not use sharding, and by doing so, Dapper says that Flow keeps transactions atomic, consistent, isolated, and durable (ACID), and allows developers to build on each others work.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003ciframe title=\"Intro to Flow with Dapper Labs\u0026#039; CEO Roham Gharegozlou\" width=\"640\" height=\"360\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/XgBLCLHdHCQ?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture\" allowfullscreen\u003e\u003c/iframe\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFlow also features upgradeable \u003cspan class=\"link\"\u003e\u003ca alt=\"What are Smart Contracts?\" href=\"https://decrypt.co/resources/smart-contracts\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003esmart contracts\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/span\u003e, allowing smart contracts to be deployed in beta and then enhanced or fixed before being finalized and made immutable.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"did-you-know\"\u003eCryptoKitties will migrate from Ethereum to Flow, with Dapper promising \u003ca href=\"https://www.cryptokitties.co/blog/post/cryptokitties-on-flow\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003enew features\u003c/a\u003e for the breedable digital cats as well as use in future games running on Flow.\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eWhats so special about Flow?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFlow is built for the kind of collectible and interactive crypto experiences that are quickly growing in prominence, and could find much larger audiences in the years to come. NBA Top Shot has already demonstrated the potential for a blockchain-driven collectibles experience to generate \u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/56965/nba-top-shot-sells-2-6-million-in-nfts-in-30-minutes\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003ehuge sums of cash\u003c/a\u003e and find \u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/60391/nba-built-for-top-shot-nft-craze\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003emajor mainstream attention\u003c/a\u003e. Thats just one experience built on top of Flow, with many more to come.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote class=\"twitter-tweet\" data-width=\"550\" data-dnt=\"true\"\u003e\n\u003cp lang=\"en\" dir=\"ltr\"\u003eRemember this dunk? \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThis Moment is the exclusive reward for the Rising Stars Challenge 1, which ends Tuesday, March 30 at 10am PT \u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCollect all 9 required Moments \u0026amp; score yourself this monster of a poster Moment from Anthony Edwards\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eMore info: \u003ca href=\"https://t.co/Rkg3ropdV1\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003ehttps://t.co/Rkg3ropdV1\u003c/a\u003e \u003ca href=\"https://t.co/HDIQdT7KN7\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003epic.twitter.com/HDIQdT7KN7\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026mdash; NBA Top Shot (@nbatopshot) \u003ca href=\"https://twitter.com/nbatopshot/status/1369460032912248834?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eMarch 10, 2021\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cscript async src=\"https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"\u003e\u003c/script\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eFlow + NBA + UFC\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eNBA Top Shot has already been an enormous success, but Dapper Labs has other high-profile partners in its stable. The firm has signed deals with \u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/20479/ufc-to-put-fighters-like-conor-mcgregor-on-the-blockchain\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eUltimate Fighting Championship (UFC)\u003c/a\u003e and \u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/36223/cryptokitties-cat-in-the-hat-dr-seuss-collectibles-go-crypto\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eDr. Suess\u003c/a\u003e to develop crypto collectibles experiences along the same lines. Besides those brands, Dapper also has partners like gadget giant Samsung, game publisher Ubisoft, and Warner Music Group.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eWhat can you do with Flow?\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eRight now, as a user, you can interact with Flow via NBA Top Shot or by buying artwork from the VIV3 NFT marketplace, as well as other working apps built on the blockchain. Developers can begin using the various built-in tools to experiment with Flow and start building their own dapps.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"did-you-know\"\u003eDapper Labs \u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/37754/nba-stars-12-million-investment-cryptokitties-dapper-labs\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eraised a $12 million investment round\u003c/a\u003e in August 2020 that featured participation from several current NBA players, including Andre Iguodala and Spencer Dinwiddie.\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eWhere to buy FLOW\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eFlows native FLOW token was initially \u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/44545/cryptokitties-team-raise-18-million-in-flow-blockchain-token-sale\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eoffered to the public in October 2020\u003c/a\u003e through CoinList, but was unavailable within the United States and Canada. Tokens sold through the offering were locked up for at least a year thereafter, which means they cant be circulated until they're unlocked.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eOn the other hand, FLOW rewards paid to validators can be transferred and sold, so there is some FLOW out on the market, and some exchangeslike Kraken and Huobilet users transact FLOW. However, major exchanges like Binance and \u003cspan class=\"link\"\u003e\u003ca alt=\"Coinbase review\" href=\"https://decrypt.co/46690/coinbase-review-a-great-jumping-on-point-for-bitcoin-beginners\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eCoinbase\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/span\u003e do not currently handle FLOW.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eThe future\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eNFT collectibles \u003ca href=\"https://decrypt.co/collections/nfts\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003eblew up in a big way\u003c/a\u003e in late 2020 and early 2021, and Flow has been one of the biggest beneficiaries of that surge. Not only has Dapper Labs own NBA Top Shot been one of the most successful crypto dapps, but Flow has reported a significant \u003ca href=\"https://twitter.com/flow_blockchain/status/1368994468809048067\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"\u003euptick in developer requests\u003c/a\u003e during the early weeks of 2021. Top Shot","slug":"nba-top-shot","term_group":0,"term_taxonomy_id":30492,"taxonomy":"post_tag","description":"","parent":0,"count":14,"filter":"raw","custom_fields":{"i18n":{"hreflang_items":[],"language":{"language_code":"en","locale":"en_US","text_direction":false,"display_name":"English","native_name":"English","different_language":false}},"yoast":{"metatitle":"","metadesc":"","focuskw":null,"linkdex":null,"metakeywords":null,"meta-robots-noindex":null,"meta-robots-nofollow":null,"canonical":null,"redirect":null,"opengraph-title":"","opengraph-description":"","opengraph-image":null,"twitter-title":"","twitter-description":"","twitter-image":null},"authors":[]}},{"term_id":26608,"name":"NFT","slug":"nft","term_group":0,"term_taxonomy_id":26608,"taxonomy":"post_tag","description":"","parent":0,"count":174,"filter":"raw","custom_fields":{"i18n":{"hreflang_items":[],"language":{"language_code":"en","locale":"en_US","text_direction":false,"display_name":"English","native_name":"English","different_language":false}},"yoast":{"metatitle":"","metadesc":"","focuskw":null,"linkdex":null,"metakeywords":null,"meta-robots-noindex":null,"meta-robots-nofollow":null,"canonical":null,"redirect":null,"opengraph-title":"","opengraph-description":"","opengraph-image":null,"twitter-title":"","twitter-description":"","twitter-image":null},"authors":[]}},{"term_id":29365,"name":"nfts","slug":"nfts","term_group":0,"term_taxonomy_id":29365,"taxonomy":"post_tag","description":"","parent":0,"count":62,"filter":"raw","custom_fields":{"i18n":{"hreflang_items":[],"language":{"language_code":"en","locale":"en_US","text_direction":false,"display_name":"English","native_name":"English","different_language":false}},"yoast":{"metatitle":"","metadesc":"","focuskw":null,"linkdex":null,"metakeywords":null,"meta-robots-noindex":null,"meta-robots-nofollow":null,"canonical":null,"redirect":null,"opengraph-title":"","opengraph-description":"","opengraph-image":null,"twitter-title":"","twitter-description":"","twitter-image":null},"authors":[]}},{"term_id":28568,"name":"non-fungible tokens","slug":"non-fungible-tokens","term_group":0,"term_taxonomy_id":28568,"taxonomy":"post_tag","description":"","parent":0,"count":27,"filter":"raw","custom_fields":{"i18n":{"hreflang_items":[],"language":{"language_code":"en","locale":"en_US","text_direction":false,"display_name":"English","native_name":"English","different_language":false}},"yoast":{"metatitle":"","metadesc":"","focuskw":null,"linkdex":null,"metakeywords":null,"meta-robots-noindex":null,"meta-robots-nofollow":null,"canonical":null,"redirect":null,"opengraph-title":"","opengraph-description":"","opengraph-image":null,"twitter-title":"","twitter-description":"","twitter-image":null},"authors":[]}}],"link":[]},"content_text":"When CryptoKitties, one of the very first non-fungible token (NFT) projects, brought the Ethereum blockchain to a halt in late 2017 due to immense congestion, developer Dapper Labs learned firsthand that current-gen blockchains werent built to handle such demand.\n\nRather than simply find another home for the decentralized app (dapp) or wait for Ethereum scaling solutions to mature, Dapper decided to build the kind of blockchain that it and other developers could rely on.\n\nThe result is Flow, a blockchain purpose-built to support things like NFT collectibles and large-scale crypto games.\n\n\u003eOn@flow_blockchain,CryptoKittieswilldemothefullpowerofcomposability,on-chainstorage,andcryptoforconsumerappswecanaddnewfeatures,genes,breedingcomponents,andextensibilityforthirdpartydeveloperswithoutaffectingthecoretrustofthecollectorpic.twitter.com/Yohu0dTi8q\n\u003e\n\u003eRoham(@rohamg)January26,2021\n\nCryptoKitties will soon migrate to Flow, and with the surging success of Dappers NBA Top Shot, and many other developers signing on to build with Flow amidst the NFT boom, it could prove to be one of the leading blockchains for such creations.\n\nHeres a look at what Flow is, how it works, and how to get ahold of the FLOW token.\n\nWHAT IS FLOW?\n\nFlow is a blockchain that is designed for extensive scaling without the use of sharding techniques, providing fast and low-cost transactions that make sense for dapps such as NFT marketplaces and crypto-infused video games.\n\nAs mentioned, Flow hails from Dapper Labs, which decided to solve its blockchain congestion problem head-on by building one primed for games and other interactive experiences. Dapper is now using Flow for all of its own projects, including NBA Top Shot, but its open to other developers as well.\n\n\u003eFlowissplitintoFOURnodetypestoachievedramaticimprovementsinspeedandthroughput\n\u003e\n\u003e1CollectorNodesincreaseefficiency\n\u003e2ExecutionNodesenablespeedandscale\n\u003e3VerifierNodesguaranteecorrectness\n\u003e4ConsensusNodesensuredecentralizationhttps://t.co/8zFlufRONmpic.twitter.com/7FJoEKSi7K\n\u003e\n\u003eFlowBlockchain(@flow_blockchain)December6,2020\n\nHOW DOES FLOW WORK?\n\nFlow uses a proof-of-stake model that requires validators to stake a certain number of FLOW tokens to participate in the network.\n\nHowever, the way that validation works is unique amongst blockchains as Flow splits validation tasks into four separate types of nodes: consensus, verification, execution, and collection. All four node types participate in the validation of each transaction.\n\nDapper says that splitting up the tasks makes processing transactions more efficient than on rival blockchains. Its an alternative option to sharding, or spreading out the storage and computational needs of a blockchain across numerous nodes. Flow does not use sharding, and by doing so, Dapper says that Flow keeps transactions atomic, consistent, isolated, and durable (ACID), and allows developers to build on each others work.\n\nFlow also features upgradeable smart contracts, allowing smart contracts to be deployed in beta and then enhanced or fixed before being finalized and made immutable.\n\nCryptoKitties will migrate from Ethereum to Flow, with Dapper promising new features for the breedable digital cats as well as use in future games running on Flow. \n\nWHATS SO SPECIAL ABOUT FLOW?\n\nFlow is built for the kind of collectible and interactive crypto experiences that are quickly growing in prominence, and could find much larger audiences in the years to come. NBA Top Shot has already demonstrated the potential for a blockchain-driven collectibles experience to generate huge sums of cash and find major mainstream attention. Thats just one experience built on top of Flow, with many more to come.\n\n\u003eRememberthisdunk?\n\u003e\n\u003eThisMomentistheexclusiverewardfortheRisingStarsChallenge1,whichendsTuesday,March30at10amPT\n\u003e\n\u003eCollectall9requiredMoments\u0026scoreyourselfthismonsterofaposterMomentfromAnthonyEdwards\n\u003e\n\u003eMoreinfo:https://t.co/Rkg3ropdV1pic.twitter.com/HDIQdT7KN7\n\u003e\n\u003eNBATopShot(@nbatopshot)March10,2021\n\nFLOW + NBA + UFC\n\nNBA Top Shot has already been an enormous success, but Dapper Labs has other high-profile partners in its stable. The firm has signed deals with Ultimate Fighting Championship (UFC) and Dr. Suess to develop crypto collectibles experiences along the same lines. Besides those brands, Dapper also has partners like gadget giant Samsung, game publisher Ubisoft, and Warner Music Group.\n\nWHAT CAN YOU DO WITH FLOW?\n\nRight now, as a user, you can interact with Flow via NBA Top Shot or by buying artwork from the VIV3 NFT marketplace, as well as other working apps built on the blockchain. Developers can begin using the various built-in tools to experiment with Flow and start building their own dapps.\n\nDapper Labs raised a $12 million investment round in August 2020 that featured participation from several current NBA players, including Andre Iguodala and Spencer Dinwiddie. \n\nWHERE TO BUY FLOW\n\nFlows native FLOW token was initially offered to the public in October 2020 through CoinList, but was unavailable within the United States and Canada. Tokens sold through the offering were locked up for at least a year thereafter, which means they cant be circulated until they're unlocked.\n\nOn the other hand, FLOW rewards paid to validators can be transferred and sold, so there is some FLOW out on the market, and some exchangeslike Kraken and Huobilet users transact FLOW. However, major exchanges like Binance and Coinbase do not currently handle FLOW.\n\nTHE FUTURE\n\nNFT collectibles blew up in a big way in late 2020 and early 2021, and Flow has been one of the biggest beneficiaries of that surge. Not only has Dapper Labs own NBA Top Shot been one of the most successful crypto dapps, but Flow has reported a significant uptick in developer requests during the early weeks of 2021. In short, NBA Top Shot has been a successful proof of concept for Dappers custom-built blockchain, and now other developers want to tap into that infrastructure.\n\n\u003eFlowdeveloperecosystemupdate\n\u003e\n\u003eSincewesharedourlastupdateaweekago,100+moredevelopersandteamshavestartedbuildingonFlow,resultingina20%+week-over-weekgrowth\n\u003e\n\u003eDontwaitonthesideline,it'stimetobuild#BuildOnFlowhttps://t.co/VahEt6nKh6pic.twitter.com/kEyMUZRJhT\n\u003e\n\u003eFlowBlockchain(@flow_blockchain)March8,2021\n\nDapper has its own additional collectibles platforms in the works, too. Flow is designed to be used for more elaborate game experiences, as well: Dapper calls it the blockchain for open worlds. On one hand, open implies decentralizationbut it may only be a matter of time before it plays host to large-scale crypto games, as well.\n","read_this_next_post_id":5692,"read_this_next_post_type":"post","social_share_img_url":"https://cdn.decrypt.co/resize/1024/height/512/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Flow-gID_6-pID_6.png","featured_image_caption":"Flow blockchain.
